investment management companies, founded in 1975 by John C. Bogle. It is renowned for pioneering low-cost index funds, which allow investors to track broad market indices with minimal fees. Vanguard’s investor-owned structure means that the company is owned by the funds it manages, aligning its interests with those of its investors. Today, Vanguard manages trillions of dollars in assets, offering a wide range of investment products including mutual funds, ETFs, and retirement plans, with a focus on long-term, passive investing strategies.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eDigital Challenge and Our Below is a summary of the key datasets:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient Profiles\u003c/strong\u003e: This includes demographic and account details such as:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient's Age\u003c/strong\u003e: The age of each client.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient's Tenure\u003c/strong\u003e: How long each client has been with Vanguard, in both years and months.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient's Balance\u003c/strong\u003e: The total balance held across all of a client's accounts with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNumber of Accounts\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of accounts the client holds with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDigital Footprints\u003c/strong\u003e: This data captures the client's online activity at each step in the client journey:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eProcess Steps\u003c/strong\u003e: The sequence of steps each client went through in their digital process (e.g., initial page, steps 1-3, and confirmation page).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDate-Time Logs\u003c/strong\u003e: Timestamps for each action taken by the client during their online session, allowing us to track the client’s progression through each step.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExperiment Roster\u003c/strong\u003e: This dataset indicates which group each client was assigned to (Control or Test), based on their unique \u003cstrong\u003eclient_id\u003c/strong\u003e. It helps us compare the performance of the Control group (traditional UI) against the Test group (new UI with contextual prompts).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eKey Performance Indicators (KPI's)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-key-performance-indicators-kpis\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Key Performance Indicators (KPI's)\" href=\"#key-performance-indicators-kpis\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe following KPIs were tracked to evaluate the effectiveness of the experiment and assess user engagement:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCompletion Rate\u003c/strong\u003e: The percentage of users who completed the process flow from start to finish. Here's how we handled the data:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eClean Datasets:\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-clean-datasets\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Clean Datasets:\" href=\"#clean-datasets\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLoad Data\u003c/strong\u003e: We begin by loading the raw data from various sources.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDrop Missing Values\u003c/strong\u003e: Any missing values in critical columns (like \u003ccode\u003eclient_id\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eprocess_step\u003c/code\u003e, etc.) are removed to ensure that we only work with complete data.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRename Columns\u003c/strong\u003e: Columns are renamed to have consistent naming conventions and be more meaningful for analysis.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRemove 'X' Gender Values\u003c/strong\u003e: Any rows with 'X' as a gender label are removed as this represents incomplete or erroneous data.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMap Gender Codes to Labels\u003c/strong\u003e: Gender codes are mapped to more readable labels (e.g., 'M' -\u0026gt; 'Male', 'F' -\u0026gt; 'Female').\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEnsure Proper DateTime Format\u003c/strong\u003e: We ensure that the \u003ccode\u003edate_time\u003c/code\u003e column is in the correct format (i.e., datetime objects), allowing for time-based analysis.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eMerge Datasets:\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-merge-datasets\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Merge Datasets:\" href=\"#merge-datasets\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMerge Demographic Datasets\u003c/strong\u003e: We combine the demographic data (client information such as age, tenure, balance) into a single dataset.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConcatenate Web Interactions Dataset\u003c/strong\u003e: The web interactions (client's steps through the online process) are merged with the demographic data based on the \u003ccode\u003eclient_id\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFinal Merge on \u003ccode\u003eclient_id\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e: After all data is cleaned and preprocessed, we merge all datasets on the common \u003ccode\u003eclient_id\u003c/code\u003e column to create a comprehensive dataset.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSegment by Experiment Below is a summary of the key datasets:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient Profiles\u003c/strong\u003e: This includes demographic and account details such as:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient's Age\u003c/strong\u003e: The age of each client.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient's Tenure\u003c/strong\u003e: How long each client has been with Vanguard, in both years and months.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClient's Balance\u003c/strong\u003e: The total balance held across all of a client's accounts with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNumber of Accounts\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of accounts the client holds with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDigital Footprints\u003c/strong\u003e: This data captures the client's online activity at each step in the client journey:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eProcess Steps\u003c/strong\u003e: The sequence of steps each client went through in their digital process (e.g., initial page, steps 1-3, and confirmation page).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDate-Time Logs\u003c/strong\u003e: Timestamps for each action taken by the client during their online session, allowing us to track the client’s progression through each step.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExperiment Roster\u003c/strong\u003e: This dataset indicates which group each client was assigned to (Control or Test), based on their unique \u003cstrong\u003eclient_id\u003c/strong\u003e. It helps us compare the performance of the Control group (traditional UI) against the Test group (new UI with contextual prompts).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eKey Performance Indicators (KPI's)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-key-performance-indicators-kpis-1\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Key Performance Indicators (KPI's)\" href=\"#key-performance-indicators-kpis-1\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe following KPIs were tracked to evaluate the effectiveness of the experiment and assess user engagement:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCompletion Rate\u003c/strong\u003e: The percentage of users who completed the process flow from start to finish. This helps to evaluate whether the new interface leads to higher engagement and successful outcomes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEngagement Metrics\u003c/strong\u003e:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLogins\u003c/strong\u003e: The frequency with which clients logged into their accounts, a measure of engagement and usage.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCalls\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of client service calls made, indicating the level of client support needed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAverage Account Balance\u003c/strong\u003e: The average balance held by clients, which provides insights into client wealth and account activity.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTenure\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of years a client has been with Vanguard, reflecting client loyalty and long-term engagement.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eGetting fields will guide your analysis, helping you uncover insights into client behavior and preferences.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eclient_id\u003c/strong\u003e: A unique identifier for each client.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003evariation\u003c/strong\u003e: Denotes whether a client was part of the experiment (Control or Test).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003evisitor_id\u003c/strong\u003e: A unique ID for each client-device combination.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003evisit_id\u003c/strong\u003e: A unique ID for each web visit/session.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eprocess_step\u003c/strong\u003e: The step in the digital process that the client is engaged in.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003edate_time\u003c/strong\u003e: Timestamp of each web activity.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eclnt_tenure_yr\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of years a client has been with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eclnt_tenure_mnth\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of months a client has been with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eclnt_age\u003c/strong\u003e: The client’s age.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003egendr\u003c/strong\u003e: The client’s gender.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003enum_accts\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of accounts the client holds with Vanguard.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ebal\u003c/strong\u003e: The total balance across all client accounts.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ecalls_6_mnth\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of times the client reached out over the phone in the last 6 months.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003elogons_6_mnth\u003c/strong\u003e: The number of times the client logged into Vanguard’s platform over the last 6 months.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eBonus: Additional Tasks Here's how we handled the data:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eClean 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLoad Data\u003c/strong\u003e: We begin by loading the raw data from various sources.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDrop Missing Values\u003c/strong\u003e: Any missing values in critical columns (like \u003ccode\u003eclient_id\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eprocess_step\u003c/code\u003e, etc.) are removed to ensure that we only work with complete data.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRename Columns\u003c/strong\u003e: Columns are renamed to have consistent naming conventions and be more meaningful for analysis.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRemove 'X' Gender Values\u003c/strong\u003e: Any rows with 'X' as a gender label are removed as this represents incomplete or erroneous data.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMap Gender Codes to Labels\u003c/strong\u003e: Gender codes are mapped to more readable labels (e.g., 'M' -\u0026gt; 'Male', 'F' -\u0026gt; 'Female').\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEnsure Proper DateTime Format\u003c/strong\u003e: We ensure that the \u003ccode\u003edate_time\u003c/code\u003e column is in the correct format (i.e., datetime objects), allowing for time-based analysis.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" After all data is cleaned and preprocessed, we merge all datasets on the common \u003ccode\u003eclient_id\u003c/code\u003e column to create a comprehensive dataset.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSegment by Experiment dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCompletion Rate\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003cbr\u003e\nIf the \u003cstrong\u003eTest group\u003c/strong\u003e shows a higher completion rate compared to the \u003cstrong\u003eControl group\u003c/strong\u003e, it suggests that the new design has improved user engagement, making it easier for users to complete the process. This could indicate that the intuitive interface or contextual prompts helped users to feel more confident and successful in completing the steps.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTime Spent on Each Step\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003cbr\u003e\nA lower time spent at each step in the \u003cstrong\u003eTest group\u003c/strong\u003e compared to the \u003cstrong\u003eControl group\u003c/strong\u003e would suggest that the new design is more efficient. This can be interpreted as users moving through the process more quickly, likely due to the improved clarity or guidance offered by the new UI design.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eError Rates\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003cbr\u003e\nA reduction in error rates in the \u003cstrong\u003eTest group\u003c/strong\u003e would suggest that the new design is more intuitive and user-friendly. This could mean that fewer users encountered confusion or made mistakes during the process, likely because the contextual prompts and simplified steps helped guide them more effectively.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBounce Rates\u003c/strong\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\nIf the \u003cstrong\u003eTest group\u003c/strong\u003e has a lower bounce rate compared to the \u003cstrong\u003eControl group\u003c/strong\u003e, it suggests that the new design is better at keeping users engaged throughout the process. A lower bounce rate would indicate that users are more likely to stay in the process, reducing drop-offs or exits at any given step, which is a good indicator of user retention and interest.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" client tenure of those engaging with the new process the same as those engaging with the old process?\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eControl Group years\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ep-value\u003c/strong\u003e: 0.0868, \u003cstrong\u003eStatistic\u003c/strong\u003e: 1.7124 (indicates how much the means differ relative to variability)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eWe \u003cstrong\u003efail to reject the null hypothesis\u003c/strong\u003e, meaning the \u003cstrong\u003eaverage tenure is not significantly different\u003c/strong\u003e between the two groups.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe lack of significant difference in \u003cstrong\u003eaverage tenure\u003c/strong\u003e supports the validity of the A/B test results.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eHypothesis 4: Average analysis did not have many missing values, which made the initial steps of cleaning and preparation relatively straightforward. However, there were some notable issues that needed to be addressed before proceeding with any in-depth analysis:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e1. \u003cstrong\u003eFormatting Issues\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-1-formatting-issues\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 1. Formatting Issues\" href=\"#1-formatting-issues\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eInconsistent column names\u003c/strong\u003e: Several columns had different naming conventions or were not aligned across the different datasets. For example, some columns had underscores while others used camelCase, making it necessary to standardize the column names.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDate/Time formatting\u003c/strong\u003e: Some datasets had \u003cstrong\u003edate\u003c/strong\u003e or \u003cstrong\u003etimestamp\u003c/strong\u003e columns in different formats. Ensuring consistency in the \u003cstrong\u003edate_time\u003c/strong\u003e field (e.g., converting them all to a datetime format) was essential for performing time-based analyses and comparisons.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCategorical data encoding\u003c/strong\u003e: There were also inconsistencies in categorical data, such as the \u003cstrong\u003egender\u003c/strong\u003e field, where some rows had 'X' as a placeholder for missing data. These were removed or corrected as part of the cleaning process.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e2. \u003cstrong\u003eMerging Datasets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-2-merging-datasets\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 2. Merging Datasets\" href=\"#2-merging-datasets\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMerging the datasets\u003c/strong\u003e: While merging the datasets (Client Profiles, Digital Footprints, and Experiment Roster) was a relatively easy task due to well-defined unique identifiers like \u003cstrong\u003eclient_id\u003c/strong\u003e, it required careful attention to ensure that records from different sources aligned correctly.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHandling duplicates\u003c/strong\u003e: A small number of duplicate rows were found during the merging process, mostly in the \u003cstrong\u003eDigital Footprints\u003c/strong\u003e dataset, where clients had multiple entries for the same session. These were handled by deduplicating the records based on session ID and timestamps.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTime-based alignment\u003c/strong\u003e: Merging the \u003cstrong\u003eDigital Footprints\u003c/strong\u003e (pt_1 and pt_2) required aligning timestamps across the two parts of the dataset, ensuring that the interactions were in chronological order. This was relatively simple given that both parts shared a common identifier.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e3. \u003cstrong\u003eOther Considerations\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-3-other-considerations\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: 3. Other Considerations\" href=\"#3-other-considerations\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAge group categorization\u003c/strong\u003e: For better analysis and comparison, \u003cstrong\u003eage\u003c/strong\u003e data was divided into groups (e.g., under 30, 30-39, 40-49, 50+), which required the creation of custom bins to segment clients into meaningful categories.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTest/Control Group Assignment\u003c/strong\u003e: It was important to ensure that the \u003cstrong\u003eExperiment Roster\u003c/strong\u003e was properly mapped to the \u003cstrong\u003eClient Profiles\u003c/strong\u003e and \u003cstrong\u003eDigital Footprints\u003c/strong\u003e to make sure that we correctly identified which clients were assigned to the test group (new UI) and which were in the control group (old UI).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhile these issues were relatively minor and manageable, they still required careful attention to ensure the datasets were clean, merged correctly, and ready for analysis.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExperiment Evaluation\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca Ages\u003c/strong\u003e: The average age is statistically different between the Test and Control groups, as indicated by the \u003cstrong\u003ep-value of 0.0160\u003c/strong\u003e, which is less than the \u003cstrong\u003e0.05 threshold\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThis means the distribution of \u003cstrong\u003eages\u003c/strong\u003e between the two groups is \u003cstrong\u003enot uniform\u003c/strong\u003e, and age differences could potentially introduce a \u003cstrong\u003ebias in the observed completion rate\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo facilitate collaboration and ensure smooth execution throughout the project, several organizational tools and resources were used:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eProject Structure Preview\u003c/strong\u003e: We Preview\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKanban Board\u003c/strong\u003e: As the project progressed, we used a Trello board to track tasks, milestones, and progress. This helped maintain clear visibility on individual and group responsibilities.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://trello.com/b/UocZX25f/kanban-template\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTrello - Kanban Board\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCollaboration and Communication\u003c/strong\u003e: We held regular check-ins and point-of-work meetings to share progress, review work, and identify any challenges. Whenever we encountered roadblocks, we either sought assistance from team members or conducted independent and group research to resolve issues.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese tools helped streamline the workflow and fostered collaboration across different stages of the project.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eStreamlit App\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-streamlit-app\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Streamlit App\" href=\"#streamlit-app\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe development of the \u003cstrong\u003eStreamlit app\u003c/strong\u003e went through several iterations, organizational changes, and challenges before we arrived at the current structure. As the complexity of the experiment grew, it became clear that the app would need more structured navigation and interactive features to accommodate a range of analysis.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReorganization\u003c/strong\u003e: The app structure underwent several revisions, adjusting both the layout and the organization of different pages to better serve the data visualization needs. This process was iterative and required refining of how the data would be presented to users.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTechnical Issues\u003c/strong\u003e: During development, there were multiple technical hurdles related to performance, data loading, and the integration of different components. These issues required debugging and adapting the code to ensure smooth user interactions, particularly for large datasets.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eComplexity of Implementation\u003c/strong\u003e: As new features were added (such as hypothesis testing, demographic analysis, and error rate tracking), it became increasingly complex to implement and maintain the app. Despite these challenges, the final iteration provides a more robust and dynamic user experience.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 rates.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eerror_rate.py\u003c/code\u003e: Presents error rates and analysis of issues class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">About the Project</h1><a id="user-content-about-the-project" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: About the Project" href="#about-the-project"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project Overview by Ceci and Eliska</h2><a id="user-content-project-overview-by-ceci-and-eliska" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project Overview by Ceci and Eliska" href="#project-overview-by-ceci-and-eliska"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">An A/B test was conducted from 3/15/2017 to 6/20/2017 by the Vanguard team to evaluate the impact of a new digital interface.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Control Group</strong>: Clients interacted with Vanguard’s traditional online process.<br>
<strong>Test Group</strong>: Clients experienced the new, spruced-up digital interface.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project Timeline:</h3><a id="user-content-project-timeline" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project Timeline:" href="#project-timeline"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">About Vanguard Group</h2><a id="user-content-about-vanguard-group" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: About Vanguard Group" href="#about-vanguard-group"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Vanguard Group is one of the world’s largest investment management companies, founded in 1975 by John C. Bogle. It is renowned for pioneering low-cost index funds, which allow investors to track broad market indices with minimal fees. Vanguard’s investor-owned structure means that the company is owned by the funds it manages, aligning its interests with those of its investors. Today, Vanguard manages trillions of dollars in assets, offering a wide range of investment products including mutual funds, ETFs, and retirement plans, with a focus on long-term, passive investing strategies.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Digital Challenge and Our Role</h2><a id="user-content-digital-challenge-and-our-role" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Digital Challenge and Our Role" href="#digital-challenge-and-our-role"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>A/B Test Objective:</strong><br>
The goal of this experiment was to evaluate a new, modernized user interface (UI) designed to improve the online client journey through in-context prompts.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Experiment Details:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Control Group</strong>: Clients used the traditional Vanguard user interface.</li>
<li><strong>Test Group</strong>: Clients experienced the new, intuitive UI with contextual prompts designed to guide them through the online process.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Timeline:</strong><br>
The experiment took place from <strong>March 15, 2017 – June 20, 2017</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Process Flow:</strong><br>
Clients followed a sequence of steps starting from the initial page, progressing through three key steps, and finishing at the confirmation page.</p>
<p dir="auto"><em>As part of the CX (Customer Experience) team, our job was to evaluate whether the new UI leads to better user engagement and higher completion rates during online processes.</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Did the new UI lead to higher completion rates?</h3><a id="user-content-did-the-new-ui-lead-to-higher-completion-rates" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Did the new UI lead to higher completion rates?" href="#did-the-new-ui-lead-to-higher-completion-rates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The A/B test was designed to determine whether the new, intuitive UI with contextual prompts improved user engagement and completion rates compared to the traditional Vanguard user interface. The results from hypothesis testing and analysis will help answer this key question.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What Data We Have Been Working With</h2><a id="user-content-what-data-we-have-been-working-with" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What Data We Have Been Working With" href="#what-data-we-have-been-working-with"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The analysis is based on a rich set of data that provides insights into both client demographics and their digital interactions with Vanguard's platform. Below is a summary of the key datasets:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Client Profiles</strong>: This includes demographic and account details such as:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Client's Age</strong>: The age of each client.</li>
<li><strong>Client's Tenure</strong>: How long each client has been with Vanguard, in both years and months.</li>
<li><strong>Client's Balance</strong>: The total balance held across all of a client's accounts with Vanguard.</li>
<li><strong>Number of Accounts</strong>: The number of accounts the client holds with Vanguard.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Digital Footprints</strong>: This data captures the client's online activity at each step in the client journey:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Process Steps</strong>: The sequence of steps each client went through in their digital process (e.g., initial page, steps 1-3, and confirmation page).</li>
<li><strong>Date-Time Logs</strong>: Timestamps for each action taken by the client during their online session, allowing us to track the client’s progression through each step.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Experiment Roster</strong>: This dataset indicates which group each client was assigned to (Control or Test), based on their unique <strong>client_id</strong>. It helps us compare the performance of the Control group (traditional UI) against the Test group (new UI with contextual prompts).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Performance Indicators (KPI's)</h2><a id="user-content-key-performance-indicators-kpis" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Performance Indicators (KPI's)" href="#key-performance-indicators-kpis"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The following KPIs were tracked to evaluate the effectiveness of the experiment and assess user engagement:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Completion Rate</strong>: The percentage of users who completed the process flow from start to finish. This helps to evaluate whether the new interface leads to higher engagement and successful outcomes.</li>
<li><strong>Engagement Metrics</strong>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Logins</strong>: The frequency with which clients logged into their accounts, a measure of engagement and usage.</li>
<li><strong>Calls</strong>: The number of client service calls made, indicating the level of client support needed.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Average Account Balance</strong>: The average balance held by clients, which provides insights into client wealth and account activity.</li>
<li><strong>Tenure</strong>: The number of years a client has been with Vanguard, reflecting client loyalty and long-term engagement.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Getting Started</h2><a id="user-content-getting-started" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Getting Started" href="#getting-started"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Metadata</h3><a id="user-content-metadata" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Metadata" href="#metadata"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This comprehensive set of fields will guide your analysis, helping you uncover insights into client behavior and preferences.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>client_id</strong>: A unique identifier for each client.</li>
<li><strong>variation</strong>: Denotes whether a client was part of the experiment (Control or Test).</li>
<li><strong>visitor_id</strong>: A unique ID for each client-device combination.</li>
<li><strong>visit_id</strong>: A unique ID for each web visit/session.</li>
<li><strong>process_step</strong>: The step in the digital process that the client is engaged in.</li>
<li><strong>date_time</strong>: Timestamp of each web activity.</li>
<li><strong>clnt_tenure_yr</strong>: The number of years a client has been with Vanguard.</li>
<li><strong>clnt_tenure_mnth</strong>: The number of months a client has been with Vanguard.</li>
<li><strong>clnt_age</strong>: The client’s age.</li>
<li><strong>gendr</strong>: The client’s gender.</li>
<li><strong>num_accts</strong>: The number of accounts the client holds with Vanguard.</li>
<li><strong>bal</strong>: The total balance across all client accounts.</li>
<li><strong>calls_6_mnth</strong>: The number of times the client reached out over the phone in the last 6 months.</li>
<li><strong>logons_6_mnth</strong>: The number of times the client logged into Vanguard’s platform over the last 6 months.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bonus: Additional Tasks (Optional)</h3><a id="user-content-bonus-additional-tasks-optional" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bonus: Additional Tasks (Optional)" href="#bonus-additional-tasks-optional"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you have extra time after completing the core tasks, explore the following optional questions and activities:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Client Behavior Analysis</strong>: Dive deeper into the data to analyze client behavior patterns and trends.</li>
<li><strong>Power and Effect Size</strong>: Perform power analysis to determine the sample size needed for a reliable test and compute the effect size.</li>
<li><strong>Streamlit Integration</strong>: Add Streamlit widgets to your project to enable real-time analysis and visualization. Customize your app for interactivity.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Data Cleaning &amp; Merging Process</h2><a id="user-content-data-cleaning--merging-process" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Data Cleaning &amp; Merging Process" href="#data-cleaning--merging-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The data cleaning and merging process is crucial for ensuring the integrity and consistency of the dataset. Here's how we handled the data:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Clean Datasets:</h3><a id="user-content-clean-datasets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Clean Datasets:" href="#clean-datasets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Load Data</strong>: We begin by loading the raw data from various sources.</li>
<li><strong>Drop Missing Values</strong>: Any missing values in critical columns (like <code>client_id</code>, <code>process_step</code>, etc.) are removed to ensure that we only work with complete data.</li>
<li><strong>Rename Columns</strong>: Columns are renamed to have consistent naming conventions and be more meaningful for analysis.</li>
<li><strong>Remove 'X' Gender Values</strong>: Any rows with 'X' as a gender label are removed as this represents incomplete or erroneous data.</li>
<li><strong>Map Gender Codes to Labels</strong>: Gender codes are mapped to more readable labels (e.g., 'M' -&gt; 'Male', 'F' -&gt; 'Female').</li>
<li><strong>Ensure Proper DateTime Format</strong>: We ensure that the <code>date_time</code> column is in the correct format (i.e., datetime objects), allowing for time-based analysis.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Merge Datasets:</h3><a id="user-content-merge-datasets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Merge Datasets:" href="#merge-datasets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Merge Demographic Datasets</strong>: We combine the demographic data (client information such as age, tenure, balance) into a single dataset.</li>
<li><strong>Concatenate Web Interactions Dataset</strong>: The web interactions (client's steps through the online process) are merged with the demographic data based on the <code>client_id</code>.</li>
<li><strong>Final Merge on <code>client_id</code></strong>: After all data is cleaned and preprocessed, we merge all datasets on the common <code>client_id</code> column to create a comprehensive dataset.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segment by Experiment Group:</h3><a id="user-content-segment-by-experiment-group" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Segment by Experiment Group:" href="#segment-by-experiment-group"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Control and Test Groups</strong>: The dataset is split into two groups based on the <code>variation</code> column: the Control group (clients using the traditional UI) and the Test group (clients using the new UI with contextual prompts).</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sort Data:</h3><a id="user-content-sort-data" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sort Data:" href="#sort-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Sort by client_id, visit_id, process_step, and date_time</strong>: This ensures that the data is ordered by the client's journey through the process, from their first visit to the confirmation step.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Age Group Categorization:</h3><a id="user-content-age-group-categorization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Age Group Categorization:" href="#age-group-categorization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Assign Age Groups</strong>: Based on defined age bins, we categorize clients into age groups (e.g., under 30, 30-39, 40-49, 50+). This categorization is applied to the <code>df_merged</code>, as well as to the <code>control</code> and <code>test</code> datasets to facilitate age-based analysis.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Who Are Our Clients?</h2><a id="user-content-who-are-our-clients" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Who Are Our Clients?" href="#who-are-our-clients"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For demographic analysis, we worked with a pool of <strong>70,591 users</strong> after applying the cleaning and merging processes to ensure data quality.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Group with highest average tenure and balance:</h3><a id="user-content-group-with-highest-average-tenure-and-balance" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Group with highest average tenure and balance:" href="#group-with-highest-average-tenure-and-balance"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Average Persona:</h3><a id="user-content-average-persona" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Average Persona:" href="#average-persona"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
